### 3.2.2 í…Œì´ë¸” ìƒì„¸ ì„¤ê³„

#### 1. profiles (ì‚¬ìš©ìž í”„ë¡œí•„)
```sql
CREATE TABLE public.profiles (
  id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE PRIMARY KEY,
  username TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  full_name TEXT,
  avatar_url TEXT,
  is_admin BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  user_type TEXT DEFAULT 'normal', -- 'normal', 'politician'
  user_level INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
  points INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ì¸ë±ìŠ¤
CREATE INDEX idx_profiles_username ON public.profiles(username);
CREATE INDEX idx_profiles_user_type ON public.profiles(user_type);

-- RLS ì •ì±…
ALTER TABLE public.profiles ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "í”„ë¡œí•„ ì½ê¸° ê³µê°œ"
  ON public.profiles FOR SELECT
  USING (true);

CREATE POLICY "ë³¸ì¸ í”„ë¡œí•„ë§Œ ìˆ˜ì •"
  ON public.profiles FOR UPDATE
  USING (auth.uid() = id);
```

#### 2. politicians (ì •ì¹˜ì¸)
```sql
CREATE TABLE public.politicians (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  party TEXT NOT NULL,
  region TEXT NOT NULL,
  position TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'êµ­íšŒì˜ì›', 'ì‹œìž¥', 'ë„ì§€ì‚¬' ë“±
  profile_image_url TEXT,
  biography TEXT,
  official_website TEXT,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id), -- ë³¸ì¸ ì¸ì¦ ì‹œ
  avatar_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ì¸ë±ìŠ¤
CREATE INDEX idx_politicians_party ON public.politicians(party);
CREATE INDEX idx_politicians_region ON public.politicians(region);
CREATE INDEX idx_politicians_name ON public.politicians(name);

-- RLS ì •ì±…
ALTER TABLE public.politicians ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "ì •ì¹˜ì¸ ëª©ë¡ ê³µê°œ"
  ON public.politicians FOR SELECT
  USING (true);

CREATE POLICY "ê´€ë¦¬ìžë§Œ ì •ì¹˜ì¸ ìˆ˜ì •"
  ON public.politicians FOR ALL
  USING (
    EXISTS (
      SELECT 1 FROM public.profiles
      WHERE profiles.id = auth.uid() AND profiles.is_admin = true
    )
  );
```

#### 3. ai_scores (AI í‰ê°€ ì ìˆ˜)
```sql
CREATE TABLE public.ai_scores (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  politician_id INTEGER REFERENCES public.politicians(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  ai_name TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'claude', 'gpt', 'gemini', 'perplexity', 'grok'
  score REAL NOT NULL CHECK (score >= 0 AND score <= 100),
  details JSONB, -- 100ê°œ í•­ëª©ë³„ ì ìˆ˜
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  UNIQUE(politician_id, ai_name)
);

-- ì¸ë±ìŠ¤
CREATE INDEX idx_ai_scores_politician ON public.ai_scores(politician_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_ai_scores_ai_name ON public.ai_scores(ai_name);

-- RLS ì •ì±…
ALTER TABLE public.ai_scores ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "AI ì ìˆ˜ ê³µê°œ"
  ON public.ai_scores FOR SELECT
  USING (true);

CREATE POLICY "ê´€ë¦¬ìžë§Œ AI ì ìˆ˜ ê´€ë¦¬"
  ON public.ai_scores FOR ALL
  USING (
    EXISTS (
      SELECT 1 FROM public.profiles
      WHERE profiles.id = auth.uid() AND profiles.is_admin = true
    )
  );
```

#### 4. posts (ê²Œì‹œê¸€)
```sql
CREATE TABLE public.posts (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  politician_id INTEGER REFERENCES public.politicians(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  category TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'general', 'politician_post' (2ê°œ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ë¡œ ë‹¨ìˆœí™”)
  title TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(title) >= 2 AND char_length(title) <= 200),
  content TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(content) >= 10),
  view_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  upvotes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  downvotes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  is_best BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  is_concept BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ì¸ë±ìŠ¤
CREATE INDEX idx_posts_user_id ON public.posts(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_posts_politician_id ON public.posts(politician_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_posts_category ON public.posts(category);
CREATE INDEX idx_posts_created_at ON public.posts(created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_posts_upvotes ON public.posts(upvotes DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_posts_is_best ON public.posts(is_best) WHERE is_best = true;
CREATE INDEX idx_posts_is_concept ON public.posts(is_concept) WHERE is_concept = true;

-- RLS ì •ì±…
ALTER TABLE public.posts ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "ê²Œì‹œê¸€ ì½ê¸° ê³µê°œ"
  ON public.posts FOR SELECT
  USING (true);

CREATE POLICY "ë¡œê·¸ì¸ ì‚¬ìš©ìžë§Œ ìž‘ì„±"
  ON public.posts FOR INSERT
  WITH CHECK (auth.uid() = user_id);

CREATE POLICY "ë³¸ì¸ ê²Œì‹œê¸€ë§Œ ìˆ˜ì •/ì‚­ì œ"
  ON public.posts FOR UPDATE
  USING (auth.uid() = user_id OR EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM public.profiles WHERE profiles.id = auth.uid() AND profiles.is_admin = true
  ));
```

#### 5. comments (ëŒ“ê¸€)
```sql
CREATE TABLE public.comments (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  post_id INTEGER REFERENCES public.posts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  content TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(content) >= 1),
  parent_id INTEGER REFERENCES public.comments(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  upvotes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  downvotes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ì¸ë±ìŠ¤
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_post_id ON public.comments(post_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_user_id ON public.comments(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_comments_parent_id ON public.comments(parent_id);

-- RLS ì •ì±…
ALTER TABLE public.comments ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "ëŒ“ê¸€ ì½ê¸° ê³µê°œ"
  ON public.comments FOR SELECT
  USING (true);

CREATE POLICY "ë¡œê·¸ì¸ ì‚¬ìš©ìžë§Œ ëŒ“ê¸€ ìž‘ì„±"
  ON public.comments FOR INSERT
  WITH CHECK (auth.uid() = user_id);

CREATE POLICY "ë³¸ì¸ ëŒ“ê¸€ë§Œ ìˆ˜ì •/ì‚­ì œ"
  ON public.comments FOR UPDATE
  USING (auth.uid() = user_id OR EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM public.profiles WHERE profiles.id = auth.uid() AND profiles.is_admin = true
  ));
```

#### 6. votes (ì¶”ì²œ/ë¹„ì¶”ì²œ)
```sql
CREATE TABLE public.votes (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  target_type TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (target_type IN ('post', 'comment')),
  target_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  vote_type TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (vote_type IN ('up', 'down')),
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  UNIQUE(target_type, target_id, user_id)
);

-- ì¸ë±ìŠ¤
CREATE INDEX idx_votes_user_target ON public.votes(user_id, target_type, target_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_votes_target ON public.votes(target_type, target_id);

-- RLS ì •ì±…
ALTER TABLE public.votes ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "íˆ¬í‘œ ì½ê¸° ê³µê°œ"
  ON public.votes FOR SELECT
  USING (true);

CREATE POLICY "ë¡œê·¸ì¸ ì‚¬ìš©ìžë§Œ íˆ¬í‘œ"
  ON public.votes FOR INSERT
  WITH CHECK (auth.uid() = user_id);

CREATE POLICY "ë³¸ì¸ íˆ¬í‘œë§Œ ë³€ê²½"
  ON public.votes FOR UPDATE
  USING (auth.uid() = user_id);
```

#### 10. reports (ì‹ ê³ )
```sql
CREATE TABLE public.reports (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  reporter_id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  target_type TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (target_type IN ('post', 'comment', 'user')),
  target_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
  reason TEXT NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending' CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'resolved', 'dismissed')),
  admin_note TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  resolved_at TIMESTAMPTZ
);

-- ì¸ë±ìŠ¤
CREATE INDEX idx_reports_status ON public.reports(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_reports_target ON public.reports(target_type, target_id);

-- RLS ì •ì±…
ALTER TABLE public.reports ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "ê´€ë¦¬ìžë§Œ ì‹ ê³  ì¡°íšŒ"
  ON public.reports FOR SELECT
  USING (
    EXISTS (
      SELECT 1 FROM public.profiles
      WHERE profiles.id = auth.uid() AND profiles.is_admin = true
    )
  );

CREATE POLICY "ë¡œê·¸ì¸ ì‚¬ìš©ìžë§Œ ì‹ ê³ "
  ON public.reports FOR INSERT
  WITH CHECK (auth.uid() = reporter_id);
```

#### 11. user_follows (íŒ”ë¡œìš°)
```sql
CREATE TABLE public.user_follows (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  follower_id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  following_id UUID REFERENCES auth.users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  UNIQUE(follower_id, following_id),
  CHECK (follower_id != following_id)
);

-- ì¸ë±ìŠ¤

  ON public.user_follows FOR SELECT
  USING (true);

CREATE POLICY "ë³¸ì¸ë§Œ íŒ”ë¡œìš° ì¶”ê°€/ì‚­ì œ"
  ON public.user_follows FOR ALL
  USING (auth.uid() = follower_id);
```

#### 12. services (ì—°ê²° ì„œë¹„ìŠ¤ - Phase 3+)
```sql
CREATE TABLE public.services (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  category TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (category IN ('consulting', 'promotion', 'education', 'legal', 'survey')),
  company_name TEXT NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  contact_email TEXT,
  contact_phone TEXT,
  website_url TEXT,
  logo_url TEXT,
  is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ì¸ë±ìŠ¤
CREATE INDEX idx_services_category ON public.services(category);
CREATE INDEX idx_services_active ON public.services(is_active);

-- RLS ì •ì±…
ALTER TABLE public.services ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "ì„œë¹„ìŠ¤ ëª©ë¡ ê³µê°œ"
  ON public.services FOR SELECT
  USING (is_active = true);

CREATE POLICY "ê´€ë¦¬ìžë§Œ ì„œë¹„ìŠ¤ ê´€ë¦¬"
  ON public.services FOR ALL
  USING (
    EXISTS (
      SELECT 1 FROM public.profiles
      WHERE profiles.id = auth.uid() AND profiles.is_admin = true
    )
  );
```

### 3.3.3 API í˜¸ì¶œ ì˜ˆì‹œ (TypeScript)

```typescript
import { supabase } from '@/lib/supabase'

// ì •ì¹˜ì¸ ëª©ë¡ ì¡°íšŒ
const { data: politicians, error } = await supabase
  .from('politicians')
  .select('*')
  .order('name', { ascending: true })

// ì •ì¹˜ì¸ ìƒì„¸ + AI í‰ê°€
const { data: politician } = await supabase
  .from('politicians')
  .select(`
    *,
    ai_scores (
      ai_name,
      score,
      details
    )
  `)
  .eq('id', politicianId)
  .single()

// ê²Œì‹œê¸€ ëª©ë¡ (íŽ˜ì´ì§€ë„¤ì´ì…˜)
const { data: posts } = await supabase
  .from('posts')
  .select(`
    *,
    profiles (username, avatar_url),
    comments (count)
  `)
  .order('created_at', { ascending: false })
  .range(0, 19) // 0-19ë²ˆì§¸ (20ê°œ)

// ê²Œì‹œê¸€ ìž‘ì„±
const { data: post, error } = await supabase
  .from('posts')
  .insert({
    user_id: user.id,
    category: 'general',
    title: 'ì œëª©',
    content: 'ë‚´ìš©'
  })
  .select()
  .single()

// ì¶”ì²œ/ë¹„ì¶”ì²œ
const { error } = await supabase
  .from('votes')
  .upsert({
    user_id: user.id,
    target_type: 'post',
    target_id: postId,
    vote_type: 'up'
  }, {
    onConflict: 'user_id,target_type,target_id'
  })

// ì‹¤ì‹œê°„ êµ¬ë… (ìƒˆ ëŒ“ê¸€)
const subscription = supabase
  .channel('comments')
  .on('postgres_changes', {
    event: 'INSERT',
    schema: 'public',
    table: 'comments',
    filter: `post_id=eq.${postId}`
  }, (payload) => {
    console.log('ìƒˆ ëŒ“ê¸€:', payload.new)
  })
  .subscribe()
```

## 3.4 ë³´ì•ˆ ì„¤ê³„

### 3.4.1 ì¸ì¦ ë³´ì•ˆ

#### JWT í† í° ê´€ë¦¬
```typescript
// Supabaseê°€ ìžë™ìœ¼ë¡œ ê´€ë¦¬
// Access Token: 1ì‹œê°„ ë§Œë£Œ
// Refresh Token: 7ì¼ ë§Œë£Œ

// ìžë™ í† í° ê°±ì‹ 
supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((event, session) => {
  if (event === 'TOKEN_REFRESHED') {
    console.log('í† í° ê°±ì‹ ë¨')
  }

```

#### ë¹„ë°€ë²ˆí˜¸ ë³´ì•ˆ
- **í•´ì‹±**: BCrypt (Salt 10 rounds)
- **ìµœì†Œ ê¸¸ì´**: 8ìž
- **ë³µìž¡ë„**: ì˜ë¬¸ + ìˆ«ìž ì¡°í•© ê¶Œìž¥

#### ì„¸ì…˜ ê´€ë¦¬
- **ì„¸ì…˜ ì €ìž¥**: ì¿ í‚¤ (HttpOnly, Secure, SameSite=Lax)
- **ì„¸ì…˜ ë§Œë£Œ**: 7ì¼ (Refresh Token)
- **ë‹¤ì¤‘ ê¸°ê¸°**: ì§€ì›

### 3.4.2 Row Level Security (RLS)

ëª¨ë“  í…Œì´ë¸”ì— RLS ì •ì±… ì ìš©ìœ¼ë¡œ ë°ì´í„° ì ‘ê·¼ ì œì–´:

```sql
-- ì˜ˆì‹œ: ê²Œì‹œê¸€ RLS ì •ì±…

-- 1. ì½ê¸°: ëª¨ë‘ ê°€ëŠ¥
CREATE POLICY "ê²Œì‹œê¸€ ì½ê¸° ê³µê°œ"
  ON public.posts FOR SELECT
  USING (true);

-- 2. ìž‘ì„±: ë³¸ì¸ë§Œ
CREATE POLICY "ë¡œê·¸ì¸ ì‚¬ìš©ìžë§Œ ìž‘ì„±"
  ON public.posts FOR INSERT
  WITH CHECK (auth.uid() = user_id);

-- 3. ìˆ˜ì •: ë³¸ì¸ ë˜ëŠ” ê´€ë¦¬ìž
CREATE POLICY "ë³¸ì¸ ê²Œì‹œê¸€ë§Œ ìˆ˜ì •"
  ON public.posts FOR UPDATE
  USING (
    auth.uid() = user_id
    OR
    EXISTS (
      SELECT 1 FROM public.profiles
      WHERE profiles.id = auth.uid() AND profiles.is_admin = true
    )
  );

-- 4. ì‚­ì œ: ë³¸ì¸ ë˜ëŠ” ê´€ë¦¬ìž
CREATE POLICY "ë³¸ì¸ ê²Œì‹œê¸€ë§Œ ì‚­ì œ"
  ON public.posts FOR DELETE
  USING (
    auth.uid() = user_id
    OR
    EXISTS (
      SELECT 1 FROM public.profiles
      WHERE profiles.id = auth.uid() AND profiles.is_admin = true
    )
  );
```

### 3.4.3 ìž…ë ¥ ê²€ì¦

#### í”„ë¡ íŠ¸ì—”ë“œ ê²€ì¦ (Zod)

```typescript
import { z } from 'zod'

// ê²Œì‹œê¸€ ìž‘ì„± ìŠ¤í‚¤ë§ˆ
const postSchema = z.object({
  title: z.string()
    .min(2, 'ì œëª©ì€ 2ìž ì´ìƒ')
    .max(200, 'ì œëª©ì€ 200ìž ì´í•˜'),
  content: z.string()
    .min(10, 'ë‚´ìš©ì€ 10ìž ì´ìƒ'),
  category: z.enum(['general', 'politician_post']), // 2ê°œ ì¹´í…Œê³ ë¦¬ë¡œ ë‹¨ìˆœí™”
})

// ì‚¬ìš©

  console.error(result.error)
}
```

### 3.4.6 Rate Limiting

```typescript
// Supabase Edge Functionì—ì„œ Rate Limiting
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'

export async function handler(req: Request) {
  const ip = req.headers.get('x-forwarded-for')

  // IPë³„ ìš”ì²­ íšŸìˆ˜ ì œí•œ (1ë¶„ë‹¹ 60íšŒ)
  const { data: rateLimit } = await supabase
    .from('rate_limits')
    .select('count')
    .eq('ip', ip)
    .eq('minute', getCurrentMinute())
    .single()

  if (rateLimit && rateLimit.count >= 60) {
    return new Response('Too Many Requests', { status: 429 })
  }

  // ìš”ì²­ ì²˜ë¦¬...
}
```

### 3.5.4 CI/CD íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸

```yaml
# .github/workflows/deploy.yml
name: Deploy

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Install Dependencies
        run: npm install

      - name: Run Tests
        run: npm test

      - name: Build
        run: npm run build

      - name: Deploy to Vercel
        uses: amondnet/vercel-action@v20
        with:
          vercel-token: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
          vercel-org-id: ${{ secrets.ORG_ID }}
          vercel-project-id: ${{ secrets.PROJECT_ID }}

      - name: Run DB Migrations
        run: npx supabase db push
        env:
          SUPABASE_ACCESS_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SUPABASE_ACCESS_TOKEN }}
```

# Part 4: UI/UX ê¸°íš

## 4.1 ë””ìžì¸ ì›ì¹™

### 4.1.1 í•µì‹¬ ë””ìžì¸ ì›ì¹™

#### 1. ë‹¨ìˆœì„± (Simplicity)
- **ìµœì†Œí•œì˜ í´ë¦­**: ì›í•˜ëŠ” ì •ë³´ê¹Œì§€ 3í´ë¦­ ì´ë‚´
- **ëª…í™•í•œ ë ˆì´ì•„ì›ƒ**: í˜¼ëž€ìŠ¤ëŸ½ì§€ ì•Šì€ êµ¬ì¡°
- **ì¼ê´€ëœ ë””ìžì¸**: ëª¨ë“  íŽ˜ì´ì§€ ë™ì¼í•œ íŒ¨í„´

#### 2. ê°€ë…ì„± (Readability)
- **ì¶©ë¶„í•œ ì—¬ë°±**: í´ë¦¬ì•™ ìŠ¤íƒ€ì¼ì˜ ë„‰ë„‰í•œ ì—¬ë°±
- **í° í°íŠ¸**: ë³¸ë¬¸ 16px, ì œëª© 20-24px
- **ëª…í™•í•œ ê³„ì¸µ**: ì œëª©-ë¶€ì œ-ë³¸ë¬¸ êµ¬ë¶„

#### 3. ë°˜ì‘ì„± (Responsiveness)
- **ëª¨ë°”ì¼ ìš°ì„ **: ëª¨ë°”ì¼ì—ì„œ ì™„ë²½í•œ UX
- **ì ì‘í˜• ë ˆì´ì•„ì›ƒ**: í™”ë©´ í¬ê¸°ë³„ ìµœì í™”
- **í„°ì¹˜ ì¹œí™”ì **: ë²„íŠ¼ í¬ê¸° 44px ì´ìƒ

- **ìŠ¤í¬ë¦° ë¦¬ë”**: ARIA ë¼ë²¨ ì ìš©

- **ëª…í™•í•œ ì •ë³´**: ë¶ˆí•„ìš”í•œ íŒì—… ì—†ìŒ
- **ì¼ê´€ëœ í†¤**: ê³µì •í•˜ê³  ì¤‘ë¦½ì ì¸ ë””ìžì¸

### 4.1.2 ì»¬ëŸ¬ ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ

#### Primary Colors (ì£¼ ìƒ‰ìƒ)
```
íŒŒëž€ìƒ‰ (ì‹ ë¢°): #1E40AF (Blue-800)
íšŒìƒ‰ (ì¤‘ë¦½): #64748B (Slate-500)
í°ìƒ‰ (ë°°ê²½): #FFFFFF
ê²€ì€ìƒ‰ (í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸): #1E293B (Slate-900)
```

#### Semantic Colors (ì˜ë¯¸ ìƒ‰ìƒ)

### 5.6.2 Phase Gate í†µê³¼ ì¡°ê±´

```python
def can_enter_next_phase(current_phase):
    """Phase Gate í†µê³¼ ì¡°ê±´ ê²€ì¦"""

    tasks = grid.get_tasks_by_phase(current_phase)

    # 1. ëª¨ë“  Task ì™„ë£Œ í™•ì¸
    for task in tasks:
        if task['ìƒíƒœ'] != 'ì™„ë£Œ':
            return False, f"{task['ìž‘ì—…ID']} ë¯¸ì™„ë£Œ"

        # 2. Code Review ì™„ë£Œ í™•ì¸
        test_history = task['í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ë‚´ì—­']
        if "CR(" not in test_history or "@" not in test_history:
            return False, f"{task['ìž‘ì—…ID']} Code Review ë¯¸ì™„ë£Œ"

        # 3. Test ì™„ë£Œ í™•ì¸
        if "Test(" not in test_history:
            return False, f"{task['ìž‘ì—…ID']} í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë¯¸ì™„ë£Œ"

            return False, f"{task['ìž‘ì—…ID']} ë¹Œë“œ ì‹¤íŒ¨"

```

# Part 6: í’ˆì§ˆ ê´€ë¦¬

## 6.1 í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì „ëžµ

### 6.1.1 í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì²´ì¸ (CR â†’ Test â†’ Build)

í”„ë¡œì íŠ¸ ê·¸ë¦¬ë“œ ë°©ë²•ë¡  V2.0ì— ë”°ë¼ ëª¨ë“  ìž‘ì—…ì€ 3ë‹¨ê³„ ê²€ì¦ ì²´ì¸ì„ í†µê³¼í•´ì•¼ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.

```

      â†“                  â†“                â†“
  QA Agent        Test Agent         CI System
  (15 checks)     (24 test cases)    (Build Pass)
```

**CR (Code Review) ë‹¨ê³„**:
- **ë‹´ë‹¹**: QA Agent (QA-01, QA-02)
- **ê²€ì¦ í•­ëª©**: 15ê°œ ì²´í¬ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸
- **ê¸°ì¤€**: 15/15 í†µê³¼ í•„ìˆ˜

**Test ë‹¨ê³„**:
- **ë‹´ë‹¹**: Test Agent (Test-01, Test-02)
- **ê²€ì¦ í•­ëª©**: ë‹¨ìœ„/í†µí•© í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸
- **ê¸°ì¤€**: ëª¨ë“  í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ í†µê³¼
- **ê¸°ë¡ í˜•ì‹**: `Test(24/24)@Test-01`

**Build ë‹¨ê³„**:

- **ê²€ì¦ í•­ëª©**: ë¹Œë“œ ì„±ê³µ, íƒ€ìž… ì˜¤ë¥˜ ì—†ìŒ
- **ê¸°ì¤€**: Build Success
- **ê¸°ë¡ í˜•ì‹**: `Build(ì„±ê³µ)@CI`

### 6.1.2 Code Review ì²´í¬ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸ (15ê°œ í•­ëª©)

ëª¨ë“  ì½”ë“œëŠ” ë‹¤ìŒ 15ê°œ í•­ëª©ì„ ê²€ì¦ë°›ì•„ì•¼ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤:

**1. íŒŒì¼ ëª…ëª… ê·œì¹™**

### 6.2.3 ë³´ì•ˆ ê¸°ì¤€

#### 1. OWASP Top 10 ëŒ€ì‘

**A01: Broken Access Control**
- RLS (Row Level Security) ëª¨ë“  í…Œì´ë¸” ì ìš©
- ì„œë²„ ì‚¬ì´ë“œ ê¶Œí•œ ê²€ì¦

- ìµœì†Œ ê¶Œí•œ ì›ì¹™

- ê¸°ë³¸ ìžê²©ì¦ëª… ë³€ê²½

- ì„¸ì…˜ íƒ€ìž„ì•„ì›ƒ ì„¤ì •
- ë¹„ë°€ë²ˆí˜¸ ì •ì±… ê°•ì œ

## 6.3 CI/CD íŒŒì´í”„ë¼ì¸

### 6.3.1 GitHub Actions ì›Œí¬í”Œë¡œìš°

#### Workflow 1: PR Validation (PR ê²€ì¦)

**íŒŒì¼**: `.github/workflows/pr-validation.yml`

```yaml
name: PR Validation

on:
  pull_request:
    branches: [main, develop]

jobs:
  code-quality:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'
          cache: 'npm'

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Lint
        run: npm run lint

      - name: Type check
        run: npm run type-check

      - name: Format check
        run: npm run format:check

  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'
          cache: 'npm'

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Run unit tests
        run: npm run test:unit

      - name: Run integration tests
        run: npm run test:integration

      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
        with:
          files: ./coverage/coverage-final.json

  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'
          cache: 'npm'

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Build
        run: npm run build
        env:
          NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL: ${{ secrets.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL }}
          NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY: ${{ secrets.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY }}

      - name: Check bundle size
        run: npx bundlesize

  e2e:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: '20'
          cache: 'npm'

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Install Playwright
        run: npx playwright install --with-deps

      - name: Run E2E tests
        run: npm run test:e2e

      - name: Upload test results
        if: always()
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
        with:
          name: playwright-report
          path: playwright-report/

  security:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Run npm audit
        run: npm audit --audit-level=moderate

      - name: Run Snyk
        uses: snyk/actions/node@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
```

#### Workflow 2: Deploy to Production (í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜ ë°°í¬)

**íŒŒì¼**: `.github/workflows/deploy-production.yml`

```yaml
name: Deploy to Production

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Deploy to Vercel
        uses: amondnet/vercel-action@v25
        with:
          vercel-token: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
          vercel-org-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_ORG_ID }}
          vercel-project-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_PROJECT_ID }}
          vercel-args: '--prod'

      - name: Run smoke tests
        run: |
          npm ci
          npx playwright test tests/smoke/
        env:
          BASE_URL: https://politician-finder.vercel.app

      - name: Notify deployment
        uses: 8398a7/action-slack@v3
        with:
          status: ${{ job.status }}
          text: 'Production deployment completed'
          webhook_url: ${{ secrets.SLACK_WEBHOOK }}
```

### 6.3.2 ë¸Œëžœì¹˜ ì „ëžµ

```
main (í”„ë¡œë•ì…˜)
  â†‘
  â””â”€ develop (ê°œë°œ)
       â†‘
       â”œâ”€ feature/P1F3a-auth-context
       â”œâ”€ feature/P1F5b-politician-card
       â””â”€ feature/P2F1a-best-posts
```

**ë¸Œëžœì¹˜ ë„¤ì´ë°**:
- `feature/{TaskID}-{description}` (ì˜ˆ: `feature/P1F3a-auth-context`)
- `bugfix/{TaskID}-{description}` (ì˜ˆ: `bugfix/P1F3a-login-error`)
- `hotfix/{TaskID}-{description}` (ê¸´ê¸‰ ìˆ˜ì •)

**ë¨¸ì§€ ì „ëžµ**:
- Feature â†’ Develop: Squash and Merge
- Develop â†’ Main: Merge Commit (ë¦´ë¦¬ìŠ¤ ížˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ ë³´ì¡´)

### 6.3.3 ë°°í¬ ì „ëžµ

#### Preview Deployments (Vercel)
- ëª¨ë“  PRì— ìžë™ Preview URL ìƒì„±
- íŒ€ì› ë¦¬ë·° ë° í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ìš©ë„
- ìžë™ ì‚­ì œ (PR ë¨¸ì§€ í›„ 7ì¼)

#### Staging Environment

- ì‹¤ì œ ë°ì´í„°ì™€ ìœ ì‚¬í•œ í…ŒìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë°ì´í„° ì‚¬ìš©

#### 4. Custom Logging
**ë„êµ¬**: Winston + CloudWatch (ì„ íƒì )

**ë¡œê·¸ ë ˆë²¨**:
- ERROR: ì¦‰ì‹œ ëŒ€ì‘ í•„ìš”
- WARN: ì£¼ì˜ í•„ìš”
- INFO: ì¼ë°˜ ì •ë³´

**ë¡œê·¸ í˜•ì‹**:
```typescript

import winston from 'winston'

export const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: { service: 'politician-finder' },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'combined.log' }),
  ],
})
```

```typescript

 * TaskID: P{Phase}{Area}{Number}
```

```typescript
    const supabaseClient = createClient(
      Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL') ?? '',
      Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_ANON_KEY') ?? ''

    // ë¡œì§

    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ data: result }), {
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    })
  } catch (error) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: error.message }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    })
```


### 7.3.4 Database í…œí”Œë¦¿

```sql
-- P{Phase}{Area}{Number}_migration_name.sql
-- TaskID: P{Phase}{Area}{Number}
-- ìž‘ì—…: [ë§ˆì´ê·¸ë ˆì´ì…˜ ì„¤ëª…]
-- ë‹´ë‹¹AI: [AI ì´ë¦„]
-- ìƒì„±ì¼: YYYY-MM-DD

-- Create table
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS table_name (
  id UUID DEFAULT gen_random_uuid() PRIMARY KEY,
  created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Add indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_table_name_column ON table_name(column);

-- Enable RLS
ALTER TABLE table_name ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

-- Create policies
CREATE POLICY "Users can view their own data"
  ON table_name FOR SELECT
  USING (auth.uid() = user_id);
```
